72a3(phal chen): bsam gyis mi khyab ste//snang ba bskos shing phyogasu rnam par mdzes//sems can mtha' yas yongasu smin mdzad pa'i//sangs rgyas 'gro ba kun la mngon du snang //
72a4(phal chen): sems can thams cad dbang po sna tshogs te//de dag ma lus rgyal bas 'gro bar mkhyen//rnam thar 'di ni rab tu thob pa'i phyir//sna tshogs 'od 'byung lha yang rab
72a5(phal chen): dga'//rgyal bas bskal pa mtha' yas yang dag spyad//sngan chad rgyal bas chos kyang yang dag gzung //dga' ba'i yid kyis rtag tu de dag blangs//rnam thar 'di ni
72a6(phal chen): dga' ba'i 'od kyis thog/'gro ba 'dir ni thugs rje byoms bskyed cing //de bzhin gshegs pas sngan chad sems can rnams//kun gyi mya ngan mtha' yas rnam par bzlog/
72a7(phal chen): nyon mongs yongasu sbyong ba 'di la dga'//rgyal ba'i shes rab rgya che mtha' yas te//tshad med na mkhe' 'dra zhing mtshungs pa yin//de bzhin gshegs pa'i shes rab rnam
72b1(phal chen): spyod pas//mar me me tog 'odadi kyi lha dga'o//de bzhin gshegs pas 'gro mnyam sku gzugs rnams//'gro ba kun gyi bsam pa rnams la bstan//de 'dra'i tshul la rab tu sgom pa yis/
72b2(phal chen): mngon du 'ong 'phro'i lha de rab tu dga'//bsod nams rgya mtsho rgya chen mtha' yas pa//sngan chad de bzhin gshegs pas yongasu skyengs//de 'dra'i rnam par thar la rnam lci bas//
72b3(phal chen): bsod nams dpal gyi 'od de rab tu dga'//srid par rab tu rmongs pa'i sems can rnams//'khor gyur rab rib mdongs po gzigs pas na//de dag phyin phyir sangs rgyas
72b4(phal chen): mngon du byung //dri med 'od kyis rnam thar 'di thob bo//de bzhin gshegs pa'i rdzu 'phrul stobs la ltos//'gro la sprin 'dra mtha' dang dpung yang med//de dag bstan cing 'gro ba
72b5(phal chen): rnam par 'dul//spos kyi rgyal mtshan 'od kyis 'di mthong ngo //sems can rmongs pa mun pas mdongs gyur cing //rnam pa sna tshogs sgrib pas bsgribs gyur pa//sangs
72b6(phal chen): rgyas 'od kyis rnam par kun shes 'gyur//rtse mo'i 'od kyi lha ni 'di la 'jug/de la snying po byang chub kyi lha dge ba dri ma med pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa'i rgyal mtshan gyi rnam
72b7(phal chen): par thar pa ni/sangs rgyas mang po mchod pa yang dag par 'byung zhing sngon gyi smon lam gyi rgyan ston pa zhes bya'o//snying po byang chub kyi lha ri rab spo'i rin po che'i 'od kyi rnam par
73a1(phal chen): tha ra pa ni/'gro ba thams nAd dang mngon sum du byang chub kyi spyod pa yang dag par sgrub cing 'byung ba zhes bya'o//snying po byang chub kyi dbyangs kyi 'jug sgra
73a2(phal chen): sgrog nga'i rgyal mtshan gyi rnam par thar pa ni/sems can thams cad kyi bsam pa la sangs rgyas ston cing /rmi lam gyi mthar+ya sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi 'brog sgra sgrog pa zhes
73a3(phal chen): bya'o//snying po byang chub kyi lha maM tog gi char sna tshogs 'bab pa'i mig gi rnam par thar pa ni/dka' ba thams cad yongasu gtong zhing /rin po che'i char 'bebs pa'i rgyan ces
73a4(phal chen): bya'o//snying po byang chub kyi lha 'od 'phro mang po shin tu dri ma med pa'i rnam par thar pa ni/'dul ba'i sems can yongasu smin par byed cing /snying po byang chub phun sum tshogs pa
73a5(phal chen): rnam pa sna tshogs ston pa zhes bya'o//snying po byang chub kyi lha me tog gi phreng ba 'od kyi gtsug phud kyi rnam par thar pa ni/sems can thams cad kyi dbang po bzhin du chos tshul zab mo dran
73a6(phal chen): pa ston pa 'byung ba zhes bya'o//snying po byang chub kyi lha rin po che'i rgyan gyi char rab tu 'bigs pa'i rnam par thar pa ni/dga' ba yang dag par myong ba mtha' yas pa la yang dag par

73b2(phal chen): kyi rnam par thar pa ni/byang chub kyi shing yongs su zhi bas phyogs rgyas par byang ba zhes bya'o//snying po byang chub kyi lha dge ba'i lta bo sna tshogs rnam par ston pa'i 'od kyi rnam par thar
73b3(phal chen): pa ni/de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs sna tshogs yang dag par rgyu ba zhes bya'o//de nas snying po byang chub kyi lha dge ba dri ma med pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa'i rgyal mtshan gyis/sangs
73b4(phal chen): rgyas kyi mthus/snying po byang chub kyi lha'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor yod pa thams cad la rnam par bltas nas/de'i tshe tshig su bcad pa 'di dag smras so//bsgral pa mang po mtha' dang
73b5(phal chen): dpung med par//de bzhin gshegs pas ji ltar sngon spyad dran//sangs rgyas thams cad mchod cing bsgrubs pas na//de phyir de'i bsod nams na mkha'i tshad//zhing rnams mtha'
73b6(phal chen): yas tshad med 'dra med par//mi zad gtong ba'i sgo nas sngon btang bas//ri bo spo'i 'od kyi lha de ni//bder gshegs dran zhing rab tu dga' bar 'gyur//bder gshegs sprul pa
73b7(phal chen): rnam pa mthod yas pa//de dag zhing rnams kun tu rab tu rgyu//'gro bar sangs rgyas rmi lam bzhin ston cing //sprin gyi sgra dbyangs lha de rab tu dga'//mtha' yas bskal par
74a1(phal chen): dka' ba rab spyad do//dang ba'o spyan rgyas 'brel phan 'gyur//rgyu mAtsha' dun yang yongs skyon btad s+ho//de la me tog mig g+hi lnga dga'o//yon tan rin
74a2(phal chen): chen 'od 'phro mtha' yas sprin//'gro ba kun tu snying po byang chub nas//rab tu bkye ba'i sangs rgyas rdzu 'phrul gyis//'od 'phro 'gyed pa'i lus kyi lha yang dga'//sems can
74a3(phal chen): rnams kyi spyod pa rgya mtsho ste/de la rgyal po chos kyi charo yang 'bebs//de ltar mos par nem nur rnam par sel//de yis gtsug pud 'phyang ba dga' ba thob//rgyan gyi
74a4(phal chen): nAr 'bebaso mig bzang lha da ni//sems kyi skad cig gcig gis tshad med pa'o//chos don dbyings kyi bye brag mtha' yas pa/rgya mtshor tha dad yang dag shes pasdu 'jug/
74a5(phal chen): zhing rnams brjod du med pa thams cad du//'gro ba kun la sangs rgyas legs brjod pas//de phyir yon tan sangs rgyas zhing kun grags//de ni rje su spos mig lha yang
74a6(phal chen): dran//mtha' yas shing gi rnam pa sna tshogs gzugs//byang chub shing la kun kyang ma lus bstan//rdo rje sna tshogs sprin gyi lha de ni//byang chub shing la dga' bar rnam par
74a7(phal chen): lha//sangs rgyas ye shes snying po byang chub la//phyogs rnams kun tu mtha' dang mu med de//pad+ma snang zhing gisal ba'i d+ha ni//rnam thar nam yangs 'di la rang dga'o//
74b1(phal chen): sangs rgyas stobs rnams yongs dgra bsam mi khyab/snying po byang chub 'dir ni kun kyang grang //yang dag bsgrubs pas byung ba de dag ni//rnams cad sna tshogs sbyang ba'i 'od nyan to//dra/
74b2(phal chen): rkang gis 'gro rin chen dpal gyis phyag rgyu'i rnam par thar pa ni/dga' ba yongs pa rin bya che'i cher gyis/kun hU~M khyab pa zhes bya'o//rkang gis 'gro badz+rI snang ba'i 'od
74b3(phal chen): 'od kyi rnam par thar ba ni/sangs rgyas kyi sku 'od zer gyi kha dog pad+mo'i dra ba thams cad du ston pas dga' bar byed pa zhes bya'o//rkang gis 'gro me tog gcig bud kyi dpal drim
74b4(phal chen): med pa'i rnam par thar pA ni/sems kyi skad cig thams cad la de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor gyi dbyibs dang /rgyan 'byung ba zhes bya'o//rkang gis 'gro shin
74b5(phal chen): tu mdzes par gnon pa'i rnam par thar pa ni/gom pa 'dor ba thams cad du sems can mtha' yas pa 'dul ba'i rgyan tsos bya'o//rkang gis 'gro rin chen dpal gyi rgyal mtshan gyi
74b6(phal chen): rnam par thar pa ni/skad cig gcig gis pad+mo'i dre ba sna tshogs sprul pa byed cing rin po che'i char pa dang /dbyangs dang snang ba kun tu 'gyod pa zher bya'o//rlung gis 'gro dga'
74b7(phal chen): ba'i dbyangs snyan pa'i rnam par thar pa ni/dga' bo'i shugs dang nyams bde ba rgya mtsho mtha' yas pa 'byung ba zhes bya'o//rkang gis 'gro shing tsan dan gyi 'od kyi rnam par thar pa/
75a1(phal chen): ni/'khor gyi dkyil 'khor thams cad du spos kyi dad sprin du lhung ba zhes bya'o//rkang gi sa 'gro bad+mo yid du 'ong ba'i 'od kyi rnam par thar pa ni/pad+mo'i gsab
75a2(phal chen): thams cad nas yid du 'ong ba'i chos kyi dbyangs 'byung bas snang ba skyed pa zhes bya'o//rkang gis 'gro rdul gyi shugs kyi 'od kyi rnam par thar pa ni/lus kyi 'od zer rnam pa sna
75a3(phal chen): tshogs thams cad kyi dra bas sang ba 'byed pa zhes bya'o//rkang gi 'gro me tog mang po'i dkyil 'khor gyi rnam par thar pa ni/sems can thams cad la dge ba'i rtsa ba rgya

75a7(phal chen): mngon par sprul mdzad nas//zhing rnams kun tu rgyal ba gshegs mdzad pa//snang ba'i 'od zer lha des rab tu mthong //'dren pa rnams kyi chos nyid bsam mi khyab/'khor

75b2(phal chen): thams cad kun tu gshegs shing bzhud pa yis//sems can mtha' yas yongasu smin par mdzad//shin tu mdzes pas dga' bar de mthong ngo //sems can snyed kyi
75b3(phal chen): sprul pa kun 'phros pa//re re'i sku yis chos kyi dbyings kyang 'gengs//rin chen dri med 'od kyang rab tu gtong //rkang 'gro dpal gyi mtshan gyis 'di mthong ngo //de bzhin gshegs

75b7(phal chen): 'od kyi lhas mthong ngo //de bzhin gshegs sku bsam gyis mi khyab ste//gom pa gom par yon tan rgya mtsho ston//de dag sems can ji ltar mos pas mthong //rdul gyi
76a1(phal chen): 'od kyi sgras ni do mthong ngo //'jog rten mgon po rnam pad+mal rnam mang gos//phyogs ban+d+har sems can yang dag sbrul byur mdzad//me ta~Mg 'a khor nA d+ma dang

76a5(phal chen): gsung 'dul ba'i sems can thams cad la brjod cing yang dag par skul bas dga' ba 'byung ba zhes bya'o//lus kyi ri su gtogs pa'i lha rgyun bzang po'i me tog gtsug pung

76b2(phal chen): sbyin las char 'bab pa'i 'ad kyi rnam par thar pa ni/sems can thams cad kyi nyon mongs pa'i dra ma mngon par sel ba'i sbyor ba zhes bya'o//lus kyi risu gtogs pa'i lha

77a5(phal chen): bzhin du//la la bzhugs dang bzhengs dang gshegs par mthong //de yang spyad lam 'byung ba'i lhas mthong ngo //rgyal ba'i tshems kyi mtshams rnams thams

130a1(phal chen): mtsho la rnam par bltas/sangs rgyas thams cad kyi yang dag par 'byung ba'i smon lam rgya mtsho la rnam par blta ste/sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rnam par
130a2(phal chen): 'phrul pa rgya mtsho la rnam par bltas nas byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor yod pa thams cad la smras pa/kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/sangs rgyas bcom ldan
130a3(phal chen): 'das rnams kyi 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad 'du zhing 'jig pa yongs su dag pa 'byung ba'i ye shes ni bsam gyis mi khyab bo//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi
130a4(phal chen): sems can thams cad kyi las 'byung ba rgya mtsho mkhyen pa ni bsam gyis mi khyab bo//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos kyi dbyings kyi tshul rgya mtsho thams cad la rnam
130a5(phal chen): par gnas pa'i ye shes ni bsam gyis mi khyab bo//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa rgya mtsho thams cad mtha' dang dadung med par bstan pa'i me shes
130a6(phal chen): ni bsam gyis mi khyab bo//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sems can thams cad kyi las rgya mtsho rnam par dgod pa'i ye shes ni bsam gyis mi khyab bo/sangs rgyas
130a7(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bsam pa dang dad pa dang /dbang po rgya mtsho la 'jug pa'i ye shes ni bsam gyis mi khyab bo//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi thugs kyi skad
130b1(phal chen): cag gcig la/dus thams cad kyi mnyam pa nyid thugs su chud pa'i lo shos ni dasam myos mo khyab bo//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kying bzhin gshegs pa thams nA /
130b2(phal chen): rnam par 'phrul pa rgya mtsho yang dag par bstan pa'i ye shes ni bsam gyis mi khyab bo//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos kyi 'khor lo rab tu bskor ba'i ye shes ni
130b3(phal chen): bsam gyis mi khyab bo//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi rnam par dgod pa rab tu bstan pa rgya mtsho ni bsam gyis mi khyab bo//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi
130b4(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi sku rab tu bstan pa yongs su dag pa ni bsam gyis mi khyab bo//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi yon tan rgya mtsho mtha' dang dpung med pas rnam par
130b5(phal chen): snang ba ni bsam gyis mi khyab bo//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mtshan dang dpe byad bzang po yongs su dag pa ni bsam gyis mi khyab bo//sangs rgyas bcom
130b6(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams kyi 'od kyi dkyil 'khor yongs su dag bre mtha' yas pa ni bsam gyis mi khyab bo//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi 'od zer rgya mtsho kha dog
130b7(phal chen): tshogs kyi sbyin rab tu 'gyod pa mdzad pa ni bsam gyis mi khyab bo//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi dpal rin po che'i 'od 'phrob rgya mtshorna
131a1(phal chen): par rgyu ba ni bsam gyis mi khyab bo//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi gsung dang dbyangs rgya mtsho rab tu 'grub pa ni bsam gyis mi khyab go/
131a2(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi cho 'phrul rnam pa gsum yongs su bstan pas/sems can rgya mtsho yongasu smin por mdzad pa dang /gdul ba mdzad pa ni bsam gyis mi
131a3(phal chen): khyab bo//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi gdul ba rgya mtsho thams cad la brtson pa don yod pa ni bsam gyis mi khyab bo//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi
131a4(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi sa la rab tu bzhugs pa ni bsam gyis mi khyab bo//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i yul la 'jug pa ni bsam gyis mi khyab
131a5(phal chen): bo//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi byin gyi rlabs kyi mthu ni bsam gyis mi khyab bo//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi ye shes kyi spyod
131a6(phal chen): yul rnam por rgyu ba ni bsam gyis mi khyab bo//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi stobs la thub pa med pa ni bsam gyis mi khyab bo//sangs rgyas bcom ldan
131a7(phal chen): 'das rnams kyi mi bsnyengs pa zil gyis mi non pa ni bsam gyis mi khyab bo//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi ting nge 'dzin la tha mi dad par spyong
131b1(phal chen): pa ni bsam gyis mi khyab bo//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i rdzu 'phrul dang rnam par 'phrul pa ni bsam gyis mi khyab bo//sangs rgyas bcom
131b2(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams kyi mnga' chen po'i ye shes rnam par dag pa ni bsam gyis mi khyab bo//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi chos mi 'phrogs po ni bsam
131b3(phal chen): gyis mi khyab ste/de dag thams cad sangs rgyas kyi mthu dang /de bzhin gshegs pa'i byin gyi rlabs kyis byin du rlabs pas/sems can thams cad sangs rgyas kyi ye
131b4(phal chen): shes rgya mtsho la gzud pa dang /byang chub sems dpa' thams cad de bzhin gshegs pa'i yon tan rgya mtsho la rab tu 'god pa dang /'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho thams
131b5(phal chen): cad sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa thams cad kyis rnam par brgyan pa dang /bskal pa rgya mtsho thams cad du de bzhin gshegs pa'i gdung rjes su bsab pa dang /'jig
131b6(phal chen): rten gyi khams rgya mtsho thams cad du chos kyi rang bzhin gyi dkyil 'khor rab tu brjod pa dang /sems can thams cad kyi dad pa rgya mtsho tha dad pa ji lta ba bzhin du rab tu bstan pa
131b7(phal chen): dang /sems can thams cad kyi dbang po rgya mtsho la sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi tshul kun tu snang ba yang dag par bskyed pa dang /sems can thams cad kyi bsam pa
132a1(phal chen): sgrib pa'i ri thams cad rnam par gzhom pa dang /sems can thams cad kyi sems dang spyod pa rgya mtsho la 'byung ba'i lam rnam par sbyang ba dang /byang chub sems
132a2(phal chen): dpa' rgya mtsho thams cad byang chub sems dpa'i smon lam rgya mtsho la rab tu dgod pa'i phyir yang dag par bsten par bya'o//de nas byang chub sems dpo kun d+ha bzang pos 'khor
132a3(phal chen): gyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho rnams de bas kyang shin tu dga' bar bya ba dang /chos la dga' ba'i shugs thams cad rnam par 'phel bar bya ba dang /mos pa'i tshul yangs pa rgyu
132a4(phal chen): mtsho yang dag par 'byung bar bya ba dang /chos kyi dbyings kyi rang bzhin dang /snying po sgo kun dang ldan pa rnam par dag par bya ba dang /kun tu bzang po'i smon lam rgya mtsho la rab tu
132a5(phal chen): dgad par bya ba dang /ye shes kyi mig dus gsum gyi rjesu song ba yongasu sbyang ba dang /'jig rten thams cad kun nas snang bar byed pa'i snying po shes rab chen po'i rgya mtsho rnam par
132a6(phal chen): 'phel bar bya ba dang /chos kyi 'khor lo thams cad yongs su gzung ba'i gzungs kyi stobs yang dag byar bskyed pa dang /snying po byang chub thams cad du sangs rgyas kyi yul thams
132a7(phal chen): cad rab tu brjod pa dang /de bzhin gshegs pa'i chos kyi tshul snang ba'i 'od chos kyi dbyings rgya chen po dang /thams cad mkhyen pa nyid la dga' ba'i shugs rgya mtsho rnam par
132b1(phal chen): 'phel bar bya ba'i phyir/de'i tshe tshigasu bcad pa 'di dag smras so//yon tan rgya mtsho rnams kyi ye shes zab//mtha' dang dpung med des ni zhing rnams khyab//sems can bsam
132b2(phal chen): la sbyor pa ji bzhin snang //rnam par snang mdzad chos kyi 'khor lo'o//bsam gyis mi khyab rgya mtsho'i zhing yod pa//bskal pa rgya mtshor rgyal bas rnam sbyangs pas/
132b3(phal chen): sems can rgya mtsho yongs su sbyin bya'i phyir//sems can nad na rgyal ba rnam par mdzes//sems can rgya mtsho 'byung ba bsam mi khyab//sangs rgyas yul lo 'jug pa shin tu
132b4(phal chen): zab/srid pa'i gnas can dod pa chung ba yis//sangs rgyas byang chub shes par mi nus so//gzhan du gang rnams shin tu sems brtan cing //dge ba'i bshes kyis yongs
132b5(phal chen): su bzung ba dang //sangs rgyas kun gyi byin gyis brlabs pa dag/sangs rgyas ye shes 'di la rab tu 'jug/gang rnams sems dag g.yo med sgyu med cing //snying rje'i
132b6(phal chen): byasam can khong nas byams dga' dang //dad pa che zhing rlabs chen de dag ni//'di dag thos shing dga' ba thob par 'gyur//kun tu bzang po'i smon lam sa dag dang //
132b7(phal chen): chos dbyings nam pa'i dbyings su khyab pa la//gnas shing spyod pa rab tu sus spyod pa//de dag rgyal ba'i spyod yul 'di shes so//gang gis rgyal po'i rnam 'phrul 'di
133a1(phal chen): /mthong ba'i//byang chub sems dang sa thob bya logs par thob//gzhan gyi yul gyis shes par mi nus te//'di ni kun tu bzang pos rtogs pa'o//
133a2(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa kun gyis byin rlabs shing //'gro ba mtha' dang dpung med 'di dag ni//kun tu chos kyi 'khor lo rab 'khor ba//rnam par snang mdzad tshul dang
133a3(phal chen): mthu yin no//bdag gi lus su zhing rnams thams cad kyang //rab tu zhugs shing de zhugs zhing rnams kun//de dag spu che kun tu blta bar gyis//rgyal ba'i spyod yul
133a4(phal chen): shin tu bshad par bya//kun tu bzang po'i smon lam spyod pa rnams//mtha' dang dpung med mngon par sgrub pa dang //kun tu mig gi yul dang lus ldan pa//de dag
133a5(phal chen): mgon po'i spyod yul 'di nyan to//kye rgyal ba'i sras dog/bcu po 'di dag ni 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho shin tu stan pa ste/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das 'das pa
133a6(phal chen): dang /ma byon pa dang /de ltar byung ba rnams kyis gsungs so//gsung ngo //gsung bar 'gyur//bcu gang zhe na/'dri lA~M ste/'jig rten gyi khams yongs su 'byung ba'i
133a7(phal chen): tshogs kyi rgyu rkyen shin tu bstan pa dang /'di lta ste/'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho gnas pa shin tu bstan pa dang /'di lta ste/'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i dbyings dang
133b1(phal chen): rnam pa shin tu bstan pa dang /'di lta ste/'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i lhun shin tu bstan pa dang /'di lta ste/'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rgyan shin tu bstan pa dang /
133b2(phal chen): 'di lta ste/'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho yongs su dag par bya ba'i tshul shin tu bstan pa dang /'di lta ste/'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho dag tu sangs rgyas 'byung ba
133b3(phal chen): shin tu bstan pa dang /'di lta ste/'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i bskul pa'i byin gyi rlabs shin tu bstan pa dang /'di lta ste/bskal pa mtha' yas pa'i rgyud rgyu
133b4(phal chen): mtsho shin tu bstan pa dang /'di lta ste/'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsha tha mi dad pa shin tu bstan pa'o//kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho
133b5(phal chen): bcu po 'di dag la sogs pa 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho shin tu bstan pa/'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
133b6(phal chen): 'das pa dang /ma byon pa dang /da ltar byung ba rnams kyis gsungs so//gsung ngo //gsung bar 'gyur ro//kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/de la 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsha
133b7(phal chen): thams cad ni rgyu dang rkyen la dmigs pa'i sgo//'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed phrag bcus byung ngo //'byung ngo //'byung bar 'gyur ro//bcu gang
134a1(phal chen): zhe na/'di lta ste/de bzhin gshogs pa'i byin gyi rlabs dang tshe nyid rab tu thob pa dang /sems can rnams kyi las kyi tshogs dang /byang chub sems dpa'
134a2(phal chen): thams cad thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du yang dag par sgrub pa'i chos nyid deng /sems can rnams kyis kyang byang chub sems dpa' dag dang /bsod nams kyi rtsa ba skal du mthun
134a3(phal chen): pa bsngags pa dang /byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi zhing yongs su dge ba'i smon lam gyi khyad par dang /byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi spyod pas rnam par bsgrubs pa'i smon
134a4(phal chen): lam gyis mngon par bsgrubs pa dang /byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi myos pa'i dbang rnam par dag pa dang /de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba 'jig rten las
134a5(phal chen): 'dus pa dang /rgyu mthun pas mngon pa ru'i tshung rgya zhing sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul ba khyu mchog gi mthu dbyung ba dang /byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po rnams
134a6(phal chen): kyi smon lam gyis smon par 'phrul bla'i sgo'o//kye rgya lnga ba'i sras dag/de ltar rgyu dang rkyen la dmigs pa'i skye bcu po 'di dag la sog pa rgyu dang rkyen la dmigs
134a7(phal chen): pa/'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyis 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho thams cad byung ngo //'byung ngo //'byung bar 'gyur ro//de nas byang chub
134b1(phal chen): /snyems dpa' kun tu nad pos 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho 'byung ba shin tu bstan pa 'di nyid gsal bar brjod pa'i phyir/sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis brlabs kyis/de'i tshe
134b2(phal chen): tshigasu bcad po 'di dag smras so//sangs rgyas ye shes yul ni bsam yas pas//byin rlabs rnam 'phrul de dag 'di lta bu//zhing rnams rgya mtsho ba ston pa mtha' dbung
134b3(phal chen): med//rnam par snang mdzad chos kyis yongs su sbyangs//byang chub sems dpa' kun gyi bsam pa bzhin//smon lam rgya mtsho bsam yis rnam sbyangs shing //sems can
134b4(phal chen): las rnams rgya mtsho bsam yas pas//phyogs kun zhing rnams rgya mtsho thams cad 'byung //byang chub sems dpa' kun gyi rnam 'phrul dang //thams cad mkhyen pa nyid la
134b5(phal chen): 'jug pa'i blo sa//smon lam rgya mtsho thams cad mngon bsgrubs shing //na mkha'i dbyings la 'byam klas zhing 'byung ngo //spyod pa rgya mtsho mtha' dang dpung med rnams//
134b6(phal chen): spyod cing tshad med bde gshegs yul la 'jug/phyogs kyi zhing rnams rgya mtsho kun skyong zhing //bskal pa mtha' yas zhing rnams re ror spyod//sems can bsam dbyings bsam
134b7(phal chen): gyis mi khyab pa'i//las kyis zhing rnams rgya mtsho thams cad byung //nyon mongs las kyis de dag nyon mongs bcas//mos dang bsamo pas rnam pa sna tshogs gzung so//zhing
135a1(phal chen): rnams rgya mtsho rnam dag rgyun can rnams//ron chen rkus byung sna tshogs dri med pa//dang pa rgya mtsho rnam par spel du'i phyir//rgyal sras rnams ni phyogs
135a2(phal chen): bcur zhing rnams skyong //chos dbyings rdul gyi khongs su rgyal smras rnams//kun tu bzang bloni spyad pa spyod pa dag/rdul gyi khongs su mtha' yas zhing ston te//rnam dag
135a3(phal chen): mkha' bzhin mtha' dang dpung yang med//na mkha'i dbyings 'dra'i rnam 'phrul 'di 'dra ste//snying po byang chub rgyal ba'i zhabs drung na//pad+mo'i stan 'khod kha dog mtha' yas
135a4(phal chen): kun//de dag zhing bcas lus kyi nang na 'khod//skad cig sems kyis dus gsum byung ba yi//zhing 'byung tshul dang 'jug pa kun kyang ston//sangs rgyas rnams kyis dus
135a5(phal chen): gsum zhing stan pa//rnam par snang mdzad rgya mtsho'i zhing mi zad//tshul gyi khyad par mtha' yas sna tshogs pas//rdul rnams kun la mtha' yas rgyan gyi rnams//sangs
135a6(phal chen): rgyurgyas skad cig gcig lnga byin gyis rlog/rgyun gyi rnam pa tshul kun rab tu mkhyen//kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/de la gnas pa shin tu bstan pa ni 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho
135a7(phal chen): ri zhing yang 'jig rten gyi khrims rgya mtsho'i rdul can tu phra ba snyed de/'di ltar 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtshol pa ni/rgyan thams cad kyi rgya mtsho kun la rab tu gnas so//
135b1(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni na mkha'i dbyings kyi gnas la rab tu gnas so//'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni rin po che thams cad kyi 'od zer gyi rgya mtsho la rab tu
135b2(phal chen): gnas so//'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni sangs rgyas thams cad kyi 'od kyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho la rab tu gnas so//'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni rin
135b3(phal chen): bo che thams cad kyi kho dog gi mdog la rab tu gnas so//'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni sangs rgyas thams cad kyi dbyangs kyi dkyil 'khor la rab tu gnas
135b4(phal chen): so/'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni sgyu ma lta bu'i las kyis byung ba/lha ma yin dang mthu bo che lta bu'i lag na rdo rje rgya mtsho la rab tu gnas skyo//'jig rten
135b5(phal chen): gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni 'jig rten gyi dbang po thams cad kyi lus kyi gzugs brnyan rgya mtsho la rab tu gnas so//'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni byang
135b6(phal chen): chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi lus rgya mtsho la rab tu gnas so//'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i smon lam gyis byung
135b7(phal chen): bri'i rgyan rnam pa thams cad dang ldan pa'i rgya mtsho la rab tu gnas te/de dag la sogs pa 'jig rten gyi khams rab tu gnas pa shin tu bstan pa ni/'jig rten gyi khams
136a1(phal chen): rgyu ma tsho re re zhing yang 'jog rten gyi khams rgyu mad+hA rtsub shin tu phra ba skyed do//dra nus byang chub sems drung 'akun tu byung pos yang 'jig rten gyi khams ca/
136a2(phal chen): mtsho rab tu gnas pa shin tu bstan pa'i don 'di nyid yongs su bston pa'i phyir sangs rgyas kyi rjesade'i tshe tshogs bcad pa 'di dag smos s+ho//kun kyang zhing rnams rgya mtsho 'di
136a3(phal chen): dag rin chen rang bzhin dri med pa//rnam dag sna tshogs nor bu kun 'bar 'od zer rgya mtsho'i 'od ldan ltos//'di dag rgyal ba'i byin rlab rgyu yis dbyibs legs 'khor bar rnam
136a4(phal chen): par snang //de dag gis ni phyogs bcu'i na mkha'i dbyings rnams gzhi kun rab tu khyab//zhing rnams rgya mtsho la la dri med 'od can na mkha'i dbyings la gnas//snang ba'i skye
136a5(phal chen): po 'od can nor bu'i rgya mtsho dag la legs par gnas//'gro ba de dbus rgyal ba 'khor la chos kyi 'khor lo bzang po skor//'di ni sangs rgyas yul yin sems can
136a6(phal chen): chen shin tu mgu byed pa'o//lA la mye tog sgron makun tu rgyas pa'i mu tig nor bus brgyan//'od zer dra ba'i kun nas sprin 'bar spros 'phro sprin gyi 'od can te//zhing ma
136a7(phal chen): mtha' dang dbung med rgya chen bad+mo'i rgya mtsho dag la~M gnas//sangs rgyas rnams kyis rang brgyan zhing rnams 'byam klas kun kyang rab tu mdzes//zhing rnams rgyas
136b1(phal chen): 'khor dbyings rnams la la sangs rgyas byin la gnas//yangs shing rin tshun mang ldan rgyu tsho de dag byang chub sems dbus glang //ldag na rdo rje rgya mtsho mang tsho gros lha dbang lus
136b2(phal chen): la de bzhin gnas//de na bcom ldan rnam par snang ba mdzad kyi 'khor lo rtag tu 'khor//nor bu'i shing dang spos kyi 'phro'i sprin rnams mnyam pa'i dbyings la gnas//
136b3(phal chen): chu'i phung po dag dang rdo rje rgya mtsho brten la'ang de bzhin gnas//la la gos dang brag dang rgyal mtshan me tog sna tshogs rgya mtsho dag la gnas//kun+da na'ang rnam 'phrul
136b4(phal chen): 'di dag rgya chen rnam par snang mdzad ston pa mdzad//zhing rnams ring dang thung dang gleng gi gzugs dang rnam pa sna tshogs te//sna tshogs rgyan can snying po dri ma bral
136b5(phal chen): yongs dag dri med snang //rnam pa sna tshogs de dge smon la ma rgya mtsho'i dbyings la rab tu gnas//sangs rgyas sprin gyis kun nas yog par rtag tu na mkha'i dbyings la
136b6(phal chen): gnas//zhing rnams rgya mtsho 'bru maklas la la spyi'i tshugs yod dang mdo la glan sa//byang chub sems dpa'i cong pan rin chen 'khor los bzung bas dag paro gnas//
136b7(phal chen): de nas sangs rgyas rnam 'phrul rgya chen thams cad kun nis rab tu snang //rin chen sang sa rgyas gsung rnams kun tu gtong ldan las kyis de dge sprul//chos kyi da
137a1(phal chen): mnyam zhing rnams 'byam klas mig yor sgyu ma dang yang 'dra//mig 'phrul rnam phye rnam dag dri med sems kyis shin tu bskyed pa ste//nam mkha'i dbyings rnams sna
137a2(phal chen): tshogs rgyan gyi snying po gnas 'gyur 'di la snang //las kyi yul ni bsam gyis mi khyab 'di dag bde bar gshegs pas bstan//skad cig sems kyis zhing rnams 'byam klas
137a3(phal chen): 'gro ba kun dang mnyam pa'i rnams//zhing rdul kun la kun tu bzang po rtag par rab tu sgrub byed cing //de na bskal pa rgya mtshor 'gro ba smin par bya phyir spyad pa spyod//chos dbyings
137a4(phal chen): rgyas par bkang ste de dag kun tu rnam 'phrul rgya che ston//rdul rnams kun na chos dbyings yangs pa'i zhing rnams rgya mtsho kun kyang gnas//sangs rgyas sprin gyis byin gyis brlabs
137a5(phal chen): pas kun kyang yog cing yongs su rgyas//ji ltar rdul phran gcig la rnam sprul de bzhin 'gro ba kun na'o//rnam par snang ba'i sangs rgyas rnam 'phrul rgya chen rab tu ston pa mdzad//

137a7(phal chen): zhing 'jig par de bzhin 'gyur//shin tu yangs pa de dge smon lam rnam sbyangs las kyis yongs su bzung //kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/de la 'jig rten gyi khams rgya
137b1(phal chen): mtsho rnams kyi dbyibs ni rnam pa sna tshogs te/'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho 'byam klas pa la la ni kun nas zlum po'o//'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho 'byam klas pa la lan

137b3(phal chen): ni kun nas 'khyil pa'i dbyibs su 'dug go/'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho 'byam klas pa la la ni 'od 'phro ba'i ri'i dbyibs su 'dug go//'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho
137b4(phal chen): 'byam klas pa la la ni shong sna tshogs kyi lhun gyi dbyibs su 'dug go/'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho 'byam klas pa la la ni me tog sna tshogs kyi dbyibs su 'dug go

138a1(phal chen): rgya mtsho 'di nyid yongs su bstan pa'i phyir/sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis brlabs kyis phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras//
138a2(phal chen): rnam pa sna tshogs rgya mtsho'i zhing la ltos//rnam gyi sna tshogs mtha' yas dbyibs su gnas//dbyibs kyis rnam par phye ba sna tshogs te//phyogs rnams kun na zhing rnams rgya mtsho snad //
138a3(phal chen): le la zlum po la la zur gsum ste//de dag la li phyogs na gru bzhir gnas//nor bu pad+mo 'khor lo yan lag brgyad//kun kyang las rnams rgya mtshos rnam par bris//rdul med
138a4(phal chen): 'od kyi dbyings dang tshul 'dzin cing //gasder las grub pa rnam phyi sna tshogs te//sgo mang mtha' yas pa nas rgyu zhing 'jug/las rnams rgya mtsho bsam pa dag pas gnas//zhing rnams
138a5(phal chen): rgya mtsho sna tshogs snying po can//na mkha' 'di la ji ltar sprin gnas bzhin//de dag rin chen mang gzhi rnam par phye//de dag kun na sangs rgyas rnam par mdzes//zhing rnams 'di kun
138a6(phal chen): sems kyis rnam par brtags//sna tshogs rgyan dang snang bas kun na gnas//rnam par 'phrul pa gzhan dang gzhan dag gis//zhing rnams rgya mtsho sangs rgyas ston pa mdzad//
138a7(phal chen): bde dang sdug bsngal myong bar gyur pa ni//rnam par dag dang nyon mongs tshul bzhin te//chos nyid 'di ni rtag tu yod pa yin//de ltar las rnams rgya mtsho bsam mi khyab//
138b1(phal chen): sgra gcig rtso la bsam gyis mi khyab zhing //thams cad rdul snyed sna tshogs dbyibs su gnas//kun na sangs rgyas rnam par snang mdzad bzhugs//'khor rnams rgya mtsho chos rnams
138b2(phal chen): rab tu ston//rdul gcig rtse la phra dang yangs pa'i rnams//thams cad rdul snyed kha dog kun dang ldan//kha dog dbyibs rnams kun kyang rnam par brtags//de dag kun na rgyal
138b3(phal chen): ba'i 'khor lo 'khor//rdul rnams kun la rab tu zhing bstan pa//de dag smon lam rnam par sbrel pa yin//na mkha'i dbyings su las kyi sprul pa ni//sna tshogs sems
138b4(phal chen): dang bsam pa rnam par brtags//sems can kun mnyam rdul rnams thams cad la//sangs rgyas rnam par 'phrul pa sprul pa dag/rnam par snang mdzad chos nyid de yin te//

138b6(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni rin po che'i rgyan thams cad kyi lhan can no//'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la lce ni rin po che gcig las rnam pa sna tshogs su bkod pa'i
138b7(phal chen): rgyan gyi lhun can no//'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni rin po che thams cad kyi 'od zer gyi lhun can no//'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni 'od kha dog sna tshogs
139a1(phal chen): kyi lhun can no//'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni rgyan thams cad kyi mdog gi lhun can no//'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni rdo rje'i gzhi mi shigs

139a7(phal chen): 'od kyi lhun can no//'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni rgyan thams cad shin tu bstan pa'i lhun can no//'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtshal la ni sems kyi rnam par
139b1(phal chen): rtog pa skad cig gis dmigs pa thams cad yongs su bstan pa'i lhun can no//'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni byang chub sems dpa'i lus kyi rin po che'i dbyibs kyi lhun can no//
139b2(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni rin po che thams cad kyi me tig gi ze ba'i lhun can ni//'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni sangs rgyas thams cad kyi gsung dbyangs rnam par
139b3(phal chen): dmigs pa'i lhun can no//de nas byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang pos/yang 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i lhun shin tu bstan pa rgya mtsho 'di nyid la rab tu gzung bar bya ba'i

139b5(phal chen): bzhin kun nas gnas//rdo rje bzhin du mi shigs sra//rin chen pad+mo rnams la gnas//la la 'od zer rang bzhin te//dag cing gzud med 'od zer 'byung //rgyan rnams

140a1(phal chen): nor bu mu tig rgyun gyi snying po thams cad rnam par 'bor//mu tig 'khor lo'i gzhi dag pa//byang chub sems dpas yongs su gang //rin chen 'od 'phro byung

143b3(phal chen): rnam par gdul ba byin gyis rlob bo//sangs rgyas 'byung ba la la ni sems can rgya mtsho mtha' yas pa rnam par gdul ba byin gyis rlob ste/de dag la sogs pa 'jig rten gyi

219a3(phal chen): rab tu byung /mos pa yangs pa'i dkyil 'khor yang yongasu dag/mi khom pa dang /ngan song dang /ngan 'gro'i g.yang sa dang /'jigs pa thams cad kyang rnam par
219a4(phal chen): bsal/lus dang sems kyi gnod pa thams cad kyang rab tu zhi/sangs rgyas mthong bas dga' ba'i shugs kyang rnam par dag/thams cad mkhyen pa nyid la rab tu

219b2(phal chen): bu gzhon nu gzi brjid chen pos/sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa mthong nas/sngon gyi dge ba'i rgyud chos bcu khong du chud par gyur to//bcu gang zhe na/'di lta ste/sangs rgyas
219b3(phal chen): thams cad kyi yon tan gyi dkyil 'khor ces bya ba'i ting 'dzin khong du chud//'di lta ste/sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi dbyings la/sgo kun nas rab tu 'jug pa zhes bya ba'i ting 'dzin/

220a2(phal chen): shes bya ba'i so so yang dag par rig pa'i ye shes chen po'i sgo khong du chud //de nas rgyal po gzhon nu gzi brjid chen po zhes bya ba de/chos kyi snang ba chen po thob nas/sangs rgyas
